####################################
# to FRANCE
# ITA/U14, SPR/U35, EGY/ARA, POL/U32, ROM/U30, YUG/U27, CZE/U31, GRE/U33, HUN/U13, BUL/U29, IND
####################################


event = { 
	id = 4000200
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { ITA U14 }

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = FRA }
		ai = FRA

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }

		#FRA hasn't ceded control of its army
		OR = {
			AND = {
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
				NOT = { year = 1940 }
			}
			AND = {
				army = { size = 150 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
				year = 1940
			}
		}
		
		OR = {
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp }
				ic = 15
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 20 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp }
				ic = 30
				army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 40 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp }
				ic = 50
				army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 80 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp }
				ic = 80
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 160 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp }
				ic = 160
				army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 10 divisions sent
				flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 20 divisions sent
				flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 40 divisions sent
				flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 80 divisions sent
				flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 160 divisions sent
				flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } }
			}
		}
	}

	name = "Supplying our allies - adjustment"
 	desc = "Our allies need help supplying their army"
	style = 0 

	date = { day = 1 month = october year = 1936 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = { 
		name = "Ok" 
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp } army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } type = extra_tc value = -15 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp } army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } type = free_supplies value = -15 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp } army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } type = trigger which = 4000291 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp } army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } type = setflag which = U14_to_FRA_10exp }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp } army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } type = extra_tc value = -15 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp } army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } type = free_supplies value = -15 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp } army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } type = trigger which = 4000291 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp } army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } type = setflag which = U14_to_FRA_20exp }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp } army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } type = extra_tc value = -30 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp } army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } type = free_supplies value = -30 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp } army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } type = trigger which = 4000292 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp } army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } type = setflag which = U14_to_FRA_40exp }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp } army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } type = extra_tc value = -60 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp } army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } type = free_supplies value = -60 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp } army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } type = trigger which = 4000293 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp } army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } type = setflag which = U14_to_FRA_80exp }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp } army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } type = extra_tc value = -120 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp } army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } type = free_supplies value = -120 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp } army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } type = trigger which = 4000294 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp } army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } type = setflag which = U14_to_FRA_160exp }
		
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } } } type = extra_tc value = 15 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } } } type = free_supplies value = 15 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } } } type = trigger which = 4000295 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_10exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } } } type = clrflag which = U14_to_FRA_10exp }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } } } type = extra_tc value = 15 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } } } type = free_supplies value = 15 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } } } type = trigger which = 4000295 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_20exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } } } type = clrflag which = U14_to_FRA_20exp }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } } } type = extra_tc value = 30 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } } } type = free_supplies value = 30 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } } } type = trigger which = 4000296 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_40exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } } } type = clrflag which = U14_to_FRA_40exp }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } } } type = extra_tc value = 60 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } } } type = free_supplies value = 60 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } } } type = trigger which = 4000297 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_80exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } } } type = clrflag which = U14_to_FRA_80exp }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } } } type = extra_tc value = 120 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } } } type = free_supplies value = 120 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } } } type = trigger which = 4000298 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_FRA_160exp NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } } } type = clrflag which = U14_to_FRA_160exp }
		
		command = { type = local_setflag which = U14_to_FRA }
	}
}

event = { 
	id = 4000202
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { EGY ARA }

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = FRA }
		ai = FRA

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }

		#FRA hasn't ceded control of its army
		OR = {
			AND = {
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
				NOT = { year = 1940 }
			}
			AND = {
				army = { size = 150 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
				year = 1940
			}
		}
		
		#No land connection to USSR or human USSR
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					control = { province = 787 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 791 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1006 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1004 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1010 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1026 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1022 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1024 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1030 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1033 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1027 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1062 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 1063 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 386 data = -3 }
					control = { province = 709 data = -3 }
				}
			}
			NOT = { ai = SOV }
		}
		
		OR = {
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = EGY_to_FRA_10exp }
				ic = 15
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 20 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = EGY_to_FRA_20exp }

				ic = 160
				army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 }

				#Not 10 divisions sent
				flag = EGY_to_FRA_10exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 20 divisions sent
				flag = EGY_to_FRA_20exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 40 divisions sent
				flag = EGY_to_FRA_40exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 80 divisions sent
				flag = EGY_to_FRA_80exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 160 divisions sent
				flag = EGY_to_FRA_160exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } }
			}
		}
	}

	name = "Supplying our allies - adjustment"
 	desc = "Our allies need help supplying their army"
	style = 0 

	date = { day = 1 month = october year = 1936 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

event = { 
	id = 4000203
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { POL U32 }

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = FRA }
		ai = FRA
		NOT = { ai = SOV }

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }
		
		OR = {
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = POL_to_FRA_10exp }
				ic = 15
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 20 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = POL_to_FRA_20exp }
				ic = 30
				army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 40 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = POL_to_FRA_40exp }
				ic = 50
				army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 80 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = POL_to_FRA_80exp }
				ic = 80
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 160 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = POL_to_FRA_160exp }
				ic = 160
				army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 10 divisions sent
				flag = POL_to_FRA_10exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 20 divisions sent
				flag = POL_to_FRA_20exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 40 divisions sent
				flag = POL_to_FRA_40exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } }
			}

				#Not 160 divisions sent
				flag = POL_to_FRA_160exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } }
			}
		}

		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = FRA }
		ai = FRA
		NOT = { ai = SOV }

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }
		
		OR = {
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = IND_to_FRA_10exp }
				ic = 15
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 20 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = IND_to_FRA_20exp }
				ic = 30
				army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 40 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = IND_to_FRA_40exp }
				ic = 50
				army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 80 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = IND_to_FRA_80exp }
				ic = 80
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 160 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = IND_to_FRA_160exp }
				ic = 160
				army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 10 divisions sent
				flag = IND_to_FRA_10exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 20 divisions sent
				flag = IND_to_FRA_20exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 50 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 30 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 40 divisions sent
				flag = IND_to_FRA_40exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 70 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 50 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 80 divisions sent
				flag = IND_to_FRA_80exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 80 } }
			}
			AND = { 
				#Not 160 divisions sent
				flag = IND_to_FRA_160exp
				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 190 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 160 } }
			}
		}
	}

 	desc = "Our allies need help supplying their army"

	id = 4000302
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { EGY ARA }

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = SOV }
		ai = SOV

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }
		
		OR = {
			#FRA ceded control of its army
			AND = {
				army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
				NOT = { year = 1940 }

event = { 
	id = 4000304
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { ROM U30 }

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = SOV }
		ai = SOV

		NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }
		
		OR = {
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = ROM_to_SOV_10exp }
				ic = 15
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }

			AND = {

				NOT = { AND = { army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 } ic = 15 } }

	persistent = yes
	tag = { GRE U33 }

		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = SOV }
		ai = SOV

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }

			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = GRE_to_SOV_10exp }

event = { 
	id = 4000320
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	tag = { ITA U14 }

	trigger = {
		local_flag = ITA_to_SOV
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				ai = yes
				atwar = yes
				alliance = { country = SOV }
				ai = SOV

				#We ceded control of our army
				NOT = { army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 0 } }
				
				#FRA ceded control of its army
				NOT = { OR = {
					AND = {
						army = { size = 110 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
						NOT = { year = 1940 }
					}
					AND = {
						army = { size = 150 type = 1 which = 0 country = FRA }
						year = 1940
					}
				} }
			}
		}
		
		OR = {
			flag = U14_to_SOV_10exp
			flag = U14_to_SOV_20exp
			flag = U14_to_SOV_40exp
			flag = U14_to_SOV_80exp
			flag = U14_to_SOV_160exp
		}
	}

	name = "Supplying our allies - abrupt end"
 	desc = "Our allies need help supplying their army"
	style = 0 

	date = { day = 1 month = october year = 1936 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = { 
		name = "Ok" 
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_SOV_10exp } type = extra_tc value = 15 }
		command = { trigger = { flag = U14_to_SOV_10exp } type = free_supplies value = 15 }

	id = 4000500
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	country = MEX

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes
		alliance = { country = ENG }
		ai = ENG

		#We ceded control of our army
		NOT = { army = { size = 20 type = 1 which = 0 } }
		
		OR = {
			#At least 10 divisions sent
			AND = { 
				NOT = { flag = MEX_to_ENG_10exp }
				ic = 15
				army = { size = 30 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 20 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = MEX_to_ENG_20exp }
				ic = 30
				army = { size = 40 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 40 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = MEX_to_ENG_40exp }
				ic = 50
				army = { size = 60 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = { 
				#At least 80 divisions sent
				NOT = { flag = MEX_to_ENG_80exp }
				ic = 80
				army = { size = 100 type = 1 which = 1 }
			}
			AND = {
